SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n// Copyright Authors of Cilium\n\npackage quota\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sync\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\tcilium_v2 \"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/logfields\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/resource\"\n)\n\n// PolicyQuotaController manages per-namespace quotas for CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.\ntype PolicyQuotaController struct {\n\tlog                logrus.FieldLogger\n\tnamespacePolicies  map[string]int\n\tmu                 sync.Mutex\n\tmaxPerNamespace    int\n\tcnpResource        resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]\n}\n\n// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tlog logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlog:               log,\n\t\tnamespacePolicies: make(map[string]int),\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:   maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tcnpResource:       cnpResource,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the controller's event loop.\nfunc (pqc *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tpqc.log.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\tdefer pqc.log.Info(\"Stopped PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\tcnpEvents := pqc.cnpResource.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-cnpEvents:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif event.Kind == resource.Sync {\n\t\t\t\tpqc.log.Debug(\"PolicyQuotaController synced\")\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr = pqc.onPolicyUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr = pqc.onPolicyDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// onPolicyUpsert handles the addition or update of a CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (pqc *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyUpsert(cnp *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tpqc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pqc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tns := cnp.Namespace\n\tpqc.namespacePolicies[ns]++\n\n\tpqc.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyName:      cnp.Name,\n\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace:    ns,\n\t\t\"policyCount\":             pqc.namespacePolicies[ns],\n\t\t\"maxPerNamespace\":         pqc.maxPerNamespace,\n\t}).Debug(\"CiliumNetworkPolicy upserted\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// onPolicyDelete handles the deletion of a CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (pqc *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyDelete(cnp *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tpqc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pqc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tns := cnp.Namespace\n\tif count, exists := pqc.namespacePolicies[ns]; exists && count > 0 {\n\t\tpqc.namespacePolicies[ns]--\n\t\tif pqc.namespacePolicies[ns] == 0 {\n\t\t\tdelete(pqc.namespacePolicies, ns)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tpqc.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyName:      cnp.Name,\n\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace:    ns,\n\t\t\"policyCount\":             pqc.namespacePolicies[ns],\n\t\t\"maxPerNamespace\":         pqc.maxPerNamespace,\n\t}).Debug(\"CiliumNetworkPolicy deleted\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CheckQuota returns an error if the namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\nfunc (pqc *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tpqc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pqc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tcount := pqc.namespacePolicies[namespace]\n\tif count >= pqc.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded for namespace %q: current=%d, max=%d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, pqc.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetNamespacePolicyCounts returns a copy of the current policy counts per namespace.\n// This method is primarily for testing purposes.\nfunc (pqc *PolicyQuotaController) GetNamespacePolicyCounts() NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tlog logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlog:               log,\n\t\tnamespacePolicies: make(map[string]int),\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:   maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tcnpResource:       cnpResource,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\tcnpEvents := pqc.cnpResource.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-cnpEvents:\n\t\t\tif !ok pqc.onPolicyDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// onPolicyUpsert handles the addition or update of a CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (pqc *PolicyQuotaController) ns)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tpqc.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyName:      cnp.Name,\n\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace:    ns,\n\t\t\"policyCount\":             pqc.namespacePolicies[ns],\n\t\t\"maxPerNamespace\":         pqc.maxPerNamespace,\n\t}).Debug(\"CiliumNetworkPolicy deleted\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CheckQuota returns an error if the namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\nfunc (pqc *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tpqc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pqc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tcount := pqc.namespacePolicies[namespace]\n\tif count >= pqc.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded for namespace %q: current=%d, max=%d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, pqc.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n//
